Grand Prix Trial Winning Decklists
==================================



 Posted in **Event Coverage**
 on July 23, 2017 






![](https://media.magic.wizards.com/styles/auth_small/public/images/person/chapman.jpg)
By Chapman Sim











The Friday before any Grand Prix is always a great time to participate in Grand Prix Trials. Not only do you get a chance to familiarize yourself with the format for the main event on Saturday and Sunday, you'll also get to win two byes if you go 5-0 in these single elimination Grand Prix Trials!


Since the *Amonkhet*/*Hour of Devastation* Limited format is still pretty new, we thought you might appreciate these decklists! Check out how these 20 players built their Sealed Decks, and discover what they included in their main deck and what they left out! Special thanks to members of the Japanese coverage team for a providing a few helping hands!  
  

Oh, by the way, Jason Chan a.k.a Amaz is in Kyoto this weekend as well! Since he received a [special invitation](http://magic.wizards.com/en/articles/archive/organized-play/amaz-comes-kyoto-plus-video-through-june-2017-05-25) to compete at Pro Tour *Hour of Devastation*, he is also in attendance at Grand Prix Kyoto this weekend and he won a Grand Prix Trial yesterday!


Great job, everyone!







#### Tetsuya Iwaki


#####
